< text>
Such an inconsistent experience coming here. I've been a customer here for just over one year.  The optometrists and eye exams have always been pleasant but my experiences with Angela who fits frames and works on the sales floor has been most of the time positive and the last time really bad.

I placed an order over the phone because I lost a pair of glasses. Ordered the exact same frames again. When I came in to get them fitted it was clear  she was irritated with my not coming  in to place the order. Then when I asked why the same glasses were $20 more expensive, she was really frustrated that I asked to see the receipt  from my last purchase. She seemed irritated that I had questions about the price difference.

I told her either way I would pay and was perfectly happy to do so, just wanted to understand the price difference. When it was clear the frame price increased this year and that was the reason, she grabbed the invoice, dropped  it at the front desk and disappeared in a rush without a word to me. It left me feeling horrible, what did I do that was so wrong? I think it was a reasonable thing to ask to compare the receipts, right?

Really bad experience and I do think that was my last visit at Mebine's office. Such a shame because I liked coming to this neighborhood, really like the optometrists who were kind with me during my difficult first experience with contacts. I just don't want to be made to feel like a huge inconvenience by Angela again. Will have to find a new place. /:

This is the same review I put on yelp</text>

< Review>
As a loyal Family Dollar customer, I would often wonder about this bright yellow neighboring restaurant that I found myself frequently parking in front of. It wasn‚Äôt until yesterday that I noticed a small line inside the establishment ‚Äî  I finally told myself, today is the day I‚Äôm going in there and finding out what this place is all about. I soon realized, this owner-operated establishment serves two purposes, convenience store and restaurant. Today my friends, I will tell you about the delicious Filipino cuisine I found myself wholeheartedly enjoying.

But first, it is important to mention that this place is CASH ONLY!

Menu:
A good selection of popular Filipino foods (QTY 6) and side options (QTY 3) that offers a la carte and combo options. You can also order 3 different tray sizes for catering.

What I ordered:
Combo 2 with 2 side

-          Main dish #1: Chichen adobo

-          Main dish #2: Beef lumpia

-          Side #1: Fried rice

-          Side #2: Pancit

Cost:
$9.50. With tax it came to $9.99.

Review:
Delicious. 10 outta 10 will order again. The star of the show: BEEF LUMPIA. It came with a side of sweet & sour sauce. It is to my understanding, the Lumpia‚Äôs are what they are known for. You can order the Lumpia‚Äôs fresh, or frozen!

What I would like to try next:
Pork bicol express

If you are like me and you are open to trying out a variety of cuisines and enjoy supporting local business, definitely give this place a try üòä< /Review>

< Review>
It's great to finally have a Filipino restaurant a little closer to home, than to travel all the way to National City! And I was really, really, happy when I got there.  The plethora of Filipino goodies were all right in front of me!! I definitely got some pandesal, cracker nuts, and some other things.. haha

For my meal, I wanted to get everything that was right in front of me.  I ended up getting half/half pancit and fried rice, adobo, sisig, and the fried fish.  And of course, got my lumpia! I loved it, almost as good as my mom's cooking! ;) Will definitely go there to get my fix again.

The staff was very friendly, and weren't stingy on the portions.  And the prices were very reasonable... they have great combos at very cheap prices. Definitely worth it! Cash only.< /Review>

Many other popular Itallian dishes are available. Sauces are full bodied, rich and flavorful, East Coast style. Servings are large.

There are two menus: vegan/gluten free and conventional. The knowledgeable and friendly servers lead you through the decision making process.  Salads are large, crisp and fresh. Hot, just out of the oven, vegan dinner rolls, at extra charge, as well as, conventional rolls are served.

And, in the tradition of the Chicago pizza restaurants, a carpet of sawdust covers the floor.

The mood is intimate, perhaps a bit romantic. Wine and beer are served. The staff is knowledgeable and friendly.

Free parking in the small lot behind the restaurant and street parking. Wheelchair accessible including bathrooms.<//review>< Pictures>

< text>
I've been coming to The Pizza Cookery for the last 40 years and it's one of my favorite restaurants with consistently excellent food and awesome service.  The atmosphere is family friendly with a good vibe, it's not pretentious or trendy and it has the charm of being a place to kick back and enjoy your meal.

My favorites are the garlic rolls, the chicken wings are better than most wing places, the 5 cheese, BBQ chicken and meat lovers thick crust are heaven, the calamari is tasty and their Antipasto salad is incredible.  They also have a nice variety of beer and wine but the best thing is you're felt rushed to eat and leave like many other busy restaurants.

This is a family run business who does everything possible to make sure you enjoy your meal.  The prices are excellent, the portions are huge, the menu has something for everyone in the family, they use fresh ingredients and they also have a great vegan and kids menu.

There may be more trendy or chic places out there, but if you're looking for a real home cooked comfort food meal that's always a step above everyone else, the Pizza Cookery is the place to go.  It's been our go to place since I was a kid.<//text>

< review>
I tried to like this place, I did. But there were so many warnings signs...

Things I liked:
- The salad.
- Price on individual combo. Less than $10 for a small pizza, salad, bread & drinks is nice!
- Not noisy, big room.

Things I disliked:
- I hate places where I have to struggle to find parking.
- They didn't honor the Yelp Deal I paid for because they said the combo I bought was already discounted (but it's printed on the menu and therefore is not an "offer," but simply a combo much like you would purchase at a fast food joint.
- The Pizza. Sauce killed it for me, tasted like they bought some premade pasta sauce and tossed it on top.
- The floor. When I first visited a pizza cookery, I thought this was cute but later I started thinking it was terribly unhygienic. Do they bother sweeping when something drops on the floor? Can you even tell?</review>

My experience was really a mixed bag of good-bad-neutral, which in itself was kind of disconcerting.

I came mid-afternoon on a weekday, so I presume the manager had the floor while waiting for the next server. She seemed bored and uninterested, and disappointingly, she actually flinched when I admitted that I'd be using a Groupon voucher (seriously, it felt like an admission‚Äîlike I'd done something wrongüòü‚Äîgoing by her countenance).

That‚Äîand the utterly disappointing garlic rolls‚Äîconstitute the "bad."

In contradistinction, the ‚Äúgoods‚Äù were d@*n good.  The garlic was fresh; the cheese was perfectly melted and the flavors robust. Also, when the scheduled server arrived, she jumped right in to her role [unlike the begrudging manager] and kindly checked in periodically.

All in all, the lesson learned is to go during peak hours.</Review>

<review>So I've lived in Encino for over 3 years now, and I'd sort of given up on finding a pizza place that was as good as my favorite LA joint. I do like Rusty's, but it's no Mulberry Street Pizza.

I dream of the big, floppy slices that you fold in half, with a slightly crispy crust, tangy/spicy sauce, gooey cheese, and lots of garlic. Little did I know that my perfect slice was right there on Figueroa Street the whole time.

It could be that most times I'm down in that area, But I lucked out last Saturday night -we needed a quick bite before a show and every other place was packed. It was open and only had one patron, so we ventured in. My slice was like the pizza I'd been dreaming of ever since I left LA. It was perfect, and I probably could have eaten half a pie if I'd had the time. My salad was also delicious with the perfect amount of what tasted like homemade dressing. My fiance got a panino sandwich with meatballs which looked really cheesy and delicious.

What made the experience even more wonderful was that we were both satisfied for only $17 total. That is unheard of in Encino.  Thanks and keep up the great service again.< /review>< Name>

<username>Shelby M<//username><date>1558147760867< /date><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
Gotta say, in the past few years, Divine Nails Spa & Beauty has really stepped up their game. They used to be nowhere near my favorite nail salon, but they're quickly rising to the top (there's a lot of nail salons in Glendora).

The inside is really nice and clean. Since they did the addition and added the second side, it's gotten way better. The interior is actually nice, and makes it seem like it's better than just some random cheap nail salon. It actually looks pretty high quality. They have really nice, new spa chairs. Gotta say, they're pretty fancy too.

The actual job they do on your nails is pretty good. I never have anything too fancy done, so I can't comment on that, but for the basics, they're pretty good.

The staff is nice and friendly. I don't think I've had a bad experience with them since they've been under new management.

It can be a little pricey, but then again, the prices of nails have gone up in the area, so that's not a huge drawback.<//Review>

In addition it seems rather peculiar that my dog now has to get sedated just for a nail trimming now when in past visits, this was not so. My dog is a service dog in training, which I told them on the first visit.

I do not expect them to know the commands, but I do expect them to treat my dog fairly.

As a Psychology Major, I would recommend alternate locations if you have other plans if only to drop your pet off for an appointment. They do not have the facilities to hold your animal if you are running late.

I will now seek alternate locations for the clinical needs of my pets.< /text>

<user>116812028306730852819< /user>< user_name>
A Dark Earth Novel</user_name>
< Text>
Here's my non-biased opinion. The burger is ok but doesn't add up to price. I went two times to make sure the first time wasn't a fluke. In the end, I feel it's just an overpriced unoriginal burger (Slightly above average taste even with all the fixings). I would say a meal (with fries & drink) is worth $10 there, but even at that price, I couldn't see myself searching this place out. It just isn't that unique. I paid upwards of $15 and was disappointed. Even Jack in the box puts a box around your burger, this place puts foil, that alone should tell you something.

I would opt for In & Out because the burger matches the value, but if i was going to shell out upwards to $15, I would opt for Bulldog Grill's burger, much better and more unique.

I would also take Red Robin over 5 guys because at the same price or less at least you get to be serviced. That's my take, I hope it helped you decide!< /Text>

< Review>
I always thought in-n-out was the best.  And, no disrespect, they are great.  However... My experience at 5 Guys was at a whole different level.
First, the"little burger" ain't little. It's very big. Bigger than most other places "giant" burger. Beware, because if you say "cheeseburger" you are getting the double, which is a mountain of meat.
And, by the way, the meat is so juicy and delicious.
Same thing for the fries. Cooked peanut oil, so very healthy. Crispy on the outside and soft on the inside. The "Little Fries" are enough for 2. Trust me on this.
If you don't leave a huge fan, you accidentally went to Burger King.</Review>

< Text>
First time at Five Guys... Last time at Five Guys... Okay, to be clear here the staff was as nice as possible, got greeted walking into the restaurant, got the friendly service explaining all of their options and menu set-up. Got an efficient order time. Everything with the staff and customer service was beyond what I can expect from this kind of restaurant so kudos to that staff here. On the other hand, I didn't think the burgers where all that great for the price I paid. Yes, you get all the toppings, but select few you have to pay for. Yes, you get free twice dip and triple salted peanuts to the power of 4(salted). Yes, free refills in their cool touch screen flavored drink machine. And that's about it. 3 stars for the awesome staff and customer service but for the price and burgers(1 combo, 1 sandwich), I didn't think it was worth it.<//Text>
